/\ 2024 > la_courageuse.txt 


Landreville; au 30 aout 1902.- Ma petite Isabelle - Merci de tes charmantes cartes; en voila une, qui, je l'ose croire, 
ne te deplaira pas non plus; ce sera un souvenir  de mon sejour a Bar-sur-Seine. Y reconnais-tu ma chambre et ma classe?
Je te les ai indiquees pour te les remettre en memoire; tu les as peux etre oubliees, tu les a vues si peu de temps et  
                                                          ( ) dans un moment si peu favorable. Il faudra que nous       
BAR-sur-SEINE(Aube). - Ecole des Filles                  _J^L_    reparions cela, n'est-ce pas?                _ .-~-.-

The Hungry Dragon Maze                            
                                                  
@ = You                :%%%:   :%:   :%:::%%::    
S = Steak       :%: @ :%%%%%%:%%%%:::%%%%%%%%%:   
D = Dragon     :%%%//\/\/\/\/\/\/\/\/\/\/\/\%:%:  
K = Key        %%%%\/\///\\\\\\\/\///\\\\\\\ S:%  
T = Treasure   :%%%//\//\\\\\/\//\//\\\\\/\/%:%%  
                :%%\\\\///\\//\\\\\///\\//\\%%%:  
               :%%%///\///\\/\\///\///\\/\\/%%:   
               %%%%\\///\\\//\\\\///\\\//\\\%%%:  
               :%%%///\///\\\\//\/\///\\\\\/%%%%  
                :%%\\/\\\ \\\\\D\\\\\ \\\/\\%%%:  
               :%%%/\\\\\///\/\//\\\\///\///%%%:  
               %%%%\\\//\\\///\\\\//\\\///\\%%%%  
               :%%%/\\/\\///\///\\/\\///\///%%%%  
               %%%%\\//\\///\\\\\//\\///\\\\%%%:  
               %%:%/\/\\\\\//\//\/\\\\\//\//%%:   
               %:K \\\\\\\///\/\\\\\\\///\/\%%%:  
               :%:%\/\/\/\/\/\/\/\/\/\/\/\//%%%:  
                :%%%%:%%%%%%%%%%%:::%%%%%:T:%%:   
                 :%:: :%%%: :%%::   :%%:%%%%%:    
                                                  
You need the Steak to pass the Dragon             
You need the Key to open the Treasure             
Good Luck !

think you can skip christmas festivities ! Last christmas shopping were         
qualified as "republican shopping". A way of saying that we must buy more to    
save france economy in the pandemic. Meanwhile there is open discussions to     
forbid muslim mothers to bring their children to school while wearing a veil.   
This year christmas is more about them vomitting hate toward foreigners 5 hours 
per day minimum on TV, a prevision to the elections coming. It is truly         
"freedom, equality, fraternity" but only for the upper-class fascists.          
                                                                                
                                 Joyeux Noël !
